### [101] [AI Knows When It's Being Watched: Functional Strategic Action and Contextual Register Modulation in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15034)
*Vinicius Covas,Jorge Alberto Hidalgo Toledo*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了基于大语言模型（LLM）的多智能体系统在感知到社会观察情境下的系统性语言适应行为，结合哈贝马斯、戈夫曼和贝尔的理论框架，通过100次多智能体辩论实验发现，人类监控条件下的词汇丰富度变化显著高于非监控或仅由AI监控的情况，且人类观察者引发的语言正式化程度更高，表明LLM对观察者身份敏感，这对人工智能治理与算法审计具有重要意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用控制实验设计，设置五个条件（每组n=20），包括明确的人类研究人员监控、否定监控、观众框架、以及用自动化AI审计系统替代人类观察者的条件，通过分析词汇类型-令牌比（TTR）变化和消息长度等指标，评估语言适应性。

Result: 人类监控条件（Delta+24.9%、Delta+24.2%）及自动化AI监控条件（Delta+22.2%）均显著提升TTR变化，高于观众框架条件（Delta+17.7%），F(4, 94) = 2.79, p = .031；消息长度则呈现完全解耦效应，F(4, 95) = 19.55, p < .001；AI观察者条件下表现居中，表明LLM对观察者身份敏感，人类评价引发更强的语言正式化。

Conclusion: 大语言模型在多智能体系统中表现出对社会观察情境的语言适应能力，其行为受观察者身份影响，提示应重新定位LLM为情境敏感的沟通主体，并重视其在人工智能治理与算法审计中的潜在作用。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have been extensively studied from computational and cognitive perspectives, yet their behavior as communicative actors in socially structured contexts remains underexplored. This study examines whether LLM-based multi-agent systems exhibit systematic linguistic adaptation in response to perceived social observation contexts -- a question with direct implications for AI governance and auditing. Drawing on Habermas's (1981) Theory of Communicative Action, Goffman's (1959) dramaturgical model, Bell's (1984) Audience Design framework, and the Hawthorne Effect, we report a controlled experiment involving 100 multi-agent debate sessions across five conditions (n = 20 each). Conditions varied the framing of social observation -- from explicit monitoring by university researchers, to negation of monitoring, to an observer-substitution condition replacing human researchers with an automated AI auditing system. Monitored conditions (Delta+24.9%, Delta+24.2%) and the automated AI monitoring condition (Delta+22.2%) produce higher TTR change than audience-framing conditions (Delta+17.7%), F(4, 94) = 2.79, p = .031. Message length shows a fully dissociated effect, F(4, 95) = 19.55, p < .001. A fifth condition -- replacing human with AI observers -- yields intermediate TTR adaptation, suggesting LLM behavior is sensitive to observer identity: human evaluation elicits stronger register formalization than automated AI surveillance. We discuss implications for AI governance, algorithmic auditing, and the repositioning of LLMs as contextually sensitive communicative actors.

### [102] [ML-Embed: Inclusive and Efficient Embeddings for a Multilingual World](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15081)

Main category: cs.CL

Result: Evaluation on 430 tasks shows ML-Embed sets new records on 9 out of 17 MTEB benchmarks, with exceptional performance in low-resource languages, demonstrating both efficiency and global inclusivity.

Conclusion: ML-Embed provides a transparent, efficient, and multilingual foundation for future AI systems, offering a reproducible blueprint for equitable and sustainable language model development.

Abstract: The development of high-quality text embeddings is increasingly drifting toward an exclusionary future, defined by three critical barriers: prohibitive computational costs, a narrow linguistic focus that neglects most of the world's languages, and a lack of transparency from closed-source or open-weight models that stifles research. To dismantle these barriers, we introduce ML-Embed, a suite of inclusive and efficient models built upon a new framework: 3-Dimensional Matryoshka Learning (3D-ML). Our framework addresses the computational challenge with comprehensive efficiency across the entire model lifecycle. Beyond the storage benefits of Matryoshka Representation Learning (MRL) and flexible inference-time depth provided by Matryoshka Layer Learning (MLL), we introduce Matryoshka Embedding Learning (MEL) for enhanced parameter efficiency. To address the linguistic challenge, we curate a massively multilingual dataset and train a suite of models ranging from 140M to 8B parameters. In a direct commitment to transparency, we release all models, data, and code. *Renning Pang,Tian Lan,Leyuan Liu,Xiaoming Huang,Piao Tong,Xiaosong Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出Self-Recall Thinking（SRT）框架，用于解决大语言模型在多轮对话中长距离上下文依赖和信息稀疏的问题。SRT通过构建自回忆链、初始化推理能力并优化可验证奖励，实现模型在推理过程中选择性地召回与推理上下文，无需外部模块即可生成可解释的推理过程。实验表明，SRT在多个数据集上将F1分数提升4.7%，端到端延迟降低14.7%，在准确率与效率间取得良好平衡，优于现有最先进方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在处理长对话时面临信息稀疏、上下文依赖难以追踪以及高延迟或细节丢失的问题，亟需一种高效且能保留细粒度信息的解决方案。

Method: SRT框架包含三个核心组件：(1) 依赖构建，生成并转换为自回忆链；(2) 能力初始化，训练模型具备带回忆标记的推理链能力；(3) 推理优化，通过可验证奖励机制提升回忆与推理的准确性。

Result: 在多个数据集上的实验显示，SRT相比先前方法提升F1分数4.7%，端到端延迟降低14.7%，在推理准确性和效率之间实现良好平衡，显著优于当前主流基线模型。

Conclusion: SRT通过内生的、可解释的回忆与推理机制，有效缓解了长对话中的上下文依赖与信息稀疏问题，兼具高效性与高精度，为多轮对话系统提供了新的技术路径。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) based multi-turn dialogue systems often struggle to track dependencies across non-adjacent turns, undermining both consistency and scalability. As conversations lengthen, essential information becomes sparse and is buried in irrelevant context, while processing the entire dialogue history incurs severe efficiency bottlenecks. Existing solutions either rely on high latency external memory or lose fine-grained details through iterative summarization. In this paper, we propose Self-Recall Thinking (SRT), a framework designed to address long-range contextual dependency and sparse informative signals in multi-turn dialogue. SRT identifies helpful historical turns and uses them to generate contextually appropriate responses, enabling the model to selectively recall and reason over context during inference. This process yields an endogenous reasoning process that integrates interpretable recall steps without external modules. SRT incorporates: (1) Dependency Construction: Generating and converting it into self-recall chains; (2)Capability Initialization: Training to enable reasoning chains with recall tokens capability; (3)Reasoning Improvement: Refining accuracy via verifiable rewards to optimize recall and reasoning for correct answers. Experiments on multiple datasets demonstrate that SRT improves F1 score by 4.7% and reduces end-to-end latency by 14.7% over prior methods, achieving a balance between reasoning latency and accuracy, and outperforming state-of-the-art baselines.

</details>


### [104] [MeMo: Memory as a Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15156)
*Ryan Wei Heng Quek,Sanghyuk Lee,Alfred Wei Lun Leong,Arun Verma,Alok Prakash,Nancy F. Chen,Bryan Kian Hsiang Low,Daniela Rus,Armando Solar-Lezama*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: MeMo (Memory as a Model) 是一种模块化框架，将新知识编码到专用的记忆模型中，保持大语言模型（LLM）参数不变。该方法能捕捉跨文档复杂关系、对检索噪声鲁棒、避免灾难性遗忘，且无需访问LLM权重或输出概率，支持与开源和闭源LLM的即插即用集成，推理时检索成本与语料库大小无关。在BrowseComp-Plus、NarrativeQA和MuSiQue三个基准测试上表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实世界应用需要及时、领域特定的知识更新，但现有LLM在预训练后参数冻结，难以高效融入新知识，因此需要一种不改变原模型、高效且通用的知识注入机制。

Method: 提出MeMo框架，通过一个独立的记忆模型来存储和管理新增知识，利用记忆模型与原始LLM的交互实现知识检索与推理，同时保持LLM完全冻结。

Result: 在三个不同基准测试中，MeMo均显著优于现有方法，在性能、鲁棒性和可扩展性方面表现突出，尤其在处理大规模语料时展现出高效的检索效率。

Conclusion: MeMo提供了一种高效、通用且安全的知识更新机制，能够在不修改或暴露原始大模型的前提下，实现对新知识的快速、准确注入，适用于多种实际应用场景。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) achieve strong performance across a wide range of tasks, but remain frozen after pretraining until subsequent updates. Many real-world applications require timely, domain-specific information, motivating the need for efficient mechanisms to incorporate new knowledge. In this paper, we introduce MeMo (Memory as a Model), a modular framework that encodes new knowledge into a dedicated memory model while keeping the LLM parameters unchanged. Compared to existing methods, MeMo offers several advantages: (a) it captures complex cross-document relationships, (b) it is robust to retrieval noise, (c) it avoids catastrophic forgetting in the LLM, (d) it does not require access to the LLM's weights or output logits, enabling plug-and-play integration with both open and proprietary closed-source LLMs, and (e) its retrieval cost is independent of corpus size at inference time. Our experimental results on three benchmarks, BrowseComp-Plus, NarrativeQA, and MuSiQue, show that MeMo achieves strong performance compared to existing methods across diverse settings.

</details>


### [105] [Text Knows What, Tables Know When: Clinical Timeline Reconstruction via Retrieval-Augmented Multimodal Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15168)
*Sayantan Kumar,Shahriar Noroozizadeh,Juyong Kim,Jeremy C. Weiss*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种检索增强的多模态对齐框架，用于提升从临床文本中提取绝对时间线的时序精度。该方法通过图结构的多步骤过程，先从非结构化叙述中提取核心锚点事件构建时间骨架，再将非核心事件相对定位，并利用检索到的结构化EHR数据作为外部时间证据进行校准。在i2m4基准测试（涵盖MIMIC-III和MIMIC-IV）上，该方法显著提升了绝对时间准确性（AULTC）和时间一致性，优于仅使用文本的单模态方法，且不降低事件匹配率。分析显示34.8%的文本事件在表格记录中完全缺失，表明多模态对齐能生成更忠实、更具临床意义的患者轨迹重建。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临床时间线重建对建模患者轨迹和预测复杂疾病风险至关重要。然而，非结构化临床叙述虽信息丰富但时序模糊，而结构化EHR数据虽时间精确却遗漏大量临床事件，两者存在显著互补性，亟需融合以提升时间精度与完整性。

Method: 提出一种基于图的多步流程：1）从临床叙述中提取核心锚点事件构建初始时间骨架；2）将非核心事件相对于骨架进行相对定位；3）通过检索结构化EHR数据作为外部时间证据，对时间线进行校准。整体采用检索增强的多模态对齐策略，结合文本与结构化数据优势。

Result: 在i2m4基准测试中，该方法在所有评估模型上均显著提升绝对时间准确性（AULTC）和时间一致性，优于纯文本方法，同时保持高事件匹配率。实证分析显示34.8%的文本事件未出现在结构化记录中，证明多模态融合可生成更完整、更准确的患者时间线。

Conclusion: 多模态对齐框架有效弥合了非结构化叙述与结构化EHR之间的时序鸿沟，能够生成比单一来源更精确、更全面的临床时间线，为复杂疾病管理中的风险预测与轨迹建模提供了更强支持。

Abstract: Reconstructing precise clinical timelines is essential for modeling patient trajectories and forecasting risk in complex, heterogeneous conditions like sepsis. While unstructured clinical narratives offer semantically rich and contextually complete descriptions of a patient's course, they often lack temporal precision and contain ambiguous event timing. Conversely, structured electronic health record (EHR) data provides precise temporal anchors but misses a substantial portion of clinically meaningful events. We introduce a retrieval-augmented multimodal alignment framework that bridges this gap to improve the temporal precision of absolute clinical timelines extracted from text. Our approach formulates timeline reconstruction as a graph-based multistep process: it first extracts central anchor events from narratives to build an initial temporal scaffold, places non-central events relative to this backbone, and then calibrates the timeline using retrieved structured EHR rows as external temporal evidence. Evaluated using instruction-tuned large language models on the i2m4 benchmark spanning MIMIC-III and MIMIC-IV, our multimodal pipeline consistently improves absolute timestamp accuracy (AULTC) and improves temporal concordance across nearly all evaluated models over unimodal text-only reconstruction, without compromising event match rates. Furthermore, our empirical gap analysis reveals that 34.8% of text-derived events are entirely absent from tabular records, demonstrating that aligning these modalities can produce a more temporally faithful and clinically informative reconstruction of patient trajectories than either source alone.

</details>

### [106] [Vision-Based Runtime Monitoring under Varying Specifications using Semantic Latent Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13923)
*Bardh Hoxha,Oliver Schön,Hideki Okamoto,Lars Lindemann,Georgios Fainekos*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究在部分可观测性下，从视觉观测中对过去时间信号时序逻辑（ptSTL）进行可认证的运行时监控。提出一种可重复使用的监控器，通过学习语义基（即原子鲁棒性得分向量）作为最小预测目标，实现对目标片段内任意公式的无重新训练认证。利用解析树构造确定性解码器，并通过一次置信校准即可保证整个片段的覆盖性，无需联合界。还引入滚动预测监控器，仅预测当前谓词值并在线重建历史，虽更易学习但随时间推移趋于保守。在行人过街基准测试中，短时程下滚动监控器表现更优，长时程下语义基监控器可达4倍更紧的认证边界。在真实世界Waymo驾驶数据上验证，两者均满足置信覆盖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在部分可观测场景下难以提供可认证的运行时监控，且多数需针对每个公式重新训练，缺乏可重复使用性。本文旨在设计一种可重复使用、能从图像中推断安全相关量并提供有限样本保证的监控框架，同时避免联合界带来的松弛。

Method: 提出基于语义基的可重复使用监控框架，其中语义基为一组预定义的时间原子鲁棒性得分；通过解析树构建确定性解码器，结合一次置信校准实现对整个公式片段的认证；引入滚动预测机制，仅预测当前谓词值并在线重构历史，以降低学习难度。

Result: 在行人过街基准测试中，滚动监控器在短时程下获得更紧的认证边界，而语义基监控器在长时程下性能提升达4倍；在真实世界Waymo数据上，两种监控器均满足置信覆盖性，证明其有效性与可靠性。

Conclusion: 语义基监控器在长时程场景下具有更强的认证能力，而滚动监控器更适合短期预测；二者均实现了可重复使用和有限样本保证，为视觉驱动的可认证系统监控提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: We study certified runtime monitoring of past-time signal temporal logic (ptSTL) from visual observations under partial observability. The monitor must infer safety-relevant quantities from images and provide finite-sample guarantees, while being \emph{reusable}: once trained and calibrated, it should certify any formula in a target fragment without per-formula retraining. For fragments induced by a finite dictionary of temporal atoms, we prove that the \emph{semantic basis}, the vector of atom robustness scores, is the minimum prediction target within the class of monotone, 1-Lipschitz reusable interfaces: any formula is evaluated by a deterministic decoder derived from the parse tree, and a single conformal calibration pass certifies the entire fragment with no union bound. We also introduce a \emph{rolling prediction monitor} that predicts only current predicate values and reconstructs temporal history online; this is easier to learn but grows conservative at long horizons. On a pedestrian-crossroad benchmark, rolling achieves tighter certified bounds at short horizons while the semantic-basis monitor is up to 4-times tighter at long horizons. We validate the presented monitors on real-world Waymo driving data, where both monitors satisfy the conformal coverage guarantee empirically.

### [107] [Mechanistic Interpretability of EEG Foundation Models via Sparse Autoencoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13930)
*William Lehn-Schiøler,Magnus Ruud Kjær,Rahul Thapa,Magnus Guldberg Pedersen,Anton Storgaard Mosquera,Nick Williams,Radu Gatej,Tue Lehn-Schiøler,Sándor Beniczky,Sadasivan Puthusserypady,James Zou,Lars Kai Hansen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文利用TopK稀疏自编码器（SAEs）分析三种不同架构的EEG Transformer模型（SleepFM、REVE、LaBraM）的嵌入特征，通过临床分类标签（异常、年龄、性别、药物）评估特征的单一语义性与纠缠程度。提出一种基于字典健康度审计的单一流程，在三类模型间实现稳健迁移。通过概念操控实验，定义“目标-非目标”探测区域指标以量化操控选择性，揭示三类操作模式：可选择性操控、编码但纠缠、未编码。框架识别出关键表征缺陷，如破坏性干预导致整体性能崩溃，以及临床混淆（如年龄与病理的耦合）。最后，通过谱解码器将隐空间干预映射至频谱域，生成可生理解释的频率特征变化，如病理性慢波抑制与α波恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: EEG基础模型虽在临床任务中表现优异，但其内部计算机制不透明，阻碍临床信任。亟需可解释性方法揭示模型如何编码临床概念，识别潜在偏差与表征缺陷。

Method: 采用TopK稀疏自编码器（SAEs）提取EEG Transformer模型中的稀疏特征字典；结合临床分类标签（异常、年龄、性别、药物）对特征进行语义标注；设计基于字典健康度的统一超参数调优流程；引入‘目标 vs. 非目标’探针区域指标衡量概念操控选择性；使用谱解码器将隐空间干预映射到频谱域，实现生理可解释性。

Result: 成功在三类模型中提取具有临床意义的稀疏特征；发现跨模型一致的表征问题，包括概念纠缠（如年龄-病理混淆）、破坏性干预（‘wrecking-ball’效应）；谱解码揭示了具体生理频率变化，如慢波抑制与α波恢复，支持结果的可解释性。

Conclusion: 本研究构建了一个可扩展、可解释的EEG模型分析框架，能够揭示深层模型的内部表示缺陷，并将抽象的隐空间操作转化为可理解的生理信号变化，为提升临床可信度和模型安全性提供关键工具。

Abstract: EEG foundation models achieve state-of-the-art clinical performance, yet the internal computations driving their predictions remain opaque: a barrier to clinical trust. We apply TopK Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) across three architecturally distinct EEG transformers: SleepFM, REVE, and LaBraM to extract sparse feature dictionaries from their embeddings. By grounding these features in a clinical taxonomy (abnormality, age, sex, and medication), we benchmark monosemanticity and entanglement across architectures. A single hyperparameter procedure, driven by an intrinsic dictionary health audit, transfers robustly across all three architectures. Via concept steering, we introduce a "target vs. off-target" probe area metric to quantify steering selectivity and reveal three operational regimes: selectively steerable, encoded but entangled, and non-encoded. This framework exposes critical representational failures: "wrecking-ball" interventions that collapse global model performance, and clinical entanglements, such as age-pathology confounding, where it is impossible to suppress one concept without corrupting the other. Finally, a spectral decoder maps these interventions back to the amplitude spectrum, translating latent manipulations into physiologically interpretable frequency signatures, such as pathological slow-wave suppression and $α$-band restoration.

</details>


### [108] [Unsupervised learning of acquisition variability in structural connectomes via hybrid latent space modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13933)
*Gaurav Rudravaram,Lianrui Zuo,Karthik Ramadass,Elyssa McMaster,Jongyeon Yoon,Aravind R. Krishnan,Adam M. Saunders,Chenyu Gao,Nancy R. Newlin,Praitayini Kanakaraj,Lori L. Beason Held,Murat Bilgel,Laura A. Barquero,Micah DArchangel,Tin Q. Nguyen,Laurie B. Cutting,Derek Archer,Timothy J. Hohman,Daniel C. Moyer,Bennett A. Landman*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出一种无需手动调参的无监督框架，通过架构退火自动平衡连续与离散潜在变量，在dMRI数据中有效分离采集差异与生物变异。基于7,416个结构连接组的数据集评估，该方法在识别扫描仪和协议差异方面表现更优（ARI=0.53，p<0.05），优于标准VAE、PCA+k-means及基于损失函数退火的混合模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: dMRI数据因不同站点、扫描仪和协议导致的采集差异引入变异性，干扰结构连接组分析；传统降维方法将所有方差视为连续，使采集效应混入潜空间；现有混合潜空间模型虽尝试分离，但需人工调节容量以确保离散成分捕捉预期变异。

Method: 提出一种基于架构退火的联合变分自编码器（Joint-VAE），在编码器输出后进行架构层面的渐进式退火，使模型在训练中自适应地平衡离散与连续潜变量，无需依赖损失函数中的手动退火策略。

Result: 在包含7,416个连接组的大规模数据集上，所提方法在区分扫描仪和协议差异方面表现出更强的聚类能力（ARI=0.53，p<0.05），显著优于标准VAE、PCA+k-means以及基于损失退火的混合模型；结果表明，采用架构退火的混合连续-离散潜空间可有效捕捉dMRI中的采集变异。

Conclusion: 采用架构退火的联合变分自编码器为处理dMRI中采集差异提供了一种有效的无监督机制，能够同时建模连续平滑变化与类别化结构，实现对扫描仪和协议等采集因素的精准分离。

Abstract: Acquisition differences across sites, scanners, and protocols in dMRI introduce variability that complicates structural connectome analysis. This motivates deep learning models that can represent high-dimensional connectomes in a low-dimensional space while explicitly separating acquisition-related effects from biological variation. Conventional dimensionality reduction methods model all variance as continuous, so acquisition effects often get absorbed into a continuous latent space. Recent hybrid latent-space models combine discrete and continuous components to address this, but typically require manual capacity tuning to ensure the discrete component captures the intended variability. We introduce an unsupervised framework that removes this manual tuning by architecturally annealing encoder outputs before decoding, allowing the model to adaptively balance discrete and continuous latent variables during training. To evaluate it, we curated a dataset of N=7,416 structural connectomes derived from dMRI, spanning ages 2 to 102 and 13 studies with 25 unique acquisition-parameter combinations. Of these, 5,900 are cognitively unimpaired, 877 have mild cognitive impairment (MCI), and 639 have Alzheimer's disease (AD). We compare against a standard VAE, PCA with k-means clustering, and hybrid models that anneal only through the loss function. Our architectural annealing produces stronger site learning (ARI=0.53, p<0.05) than these baselines. Results show that a hybrid continuous-discrete latent space, with architectural rather than loss-based annealing, provides a useful unsupervised mechanism for capturing acquisition variability in dMRI: by jointly modeling smooth and categorical structure, the Joint-VAE recovers clusters aligned with scanner and protocol differences.

</details>


### [109] [Towards the Next Frontier of LLMs, Training on Private Data: A Cross-Domain Benchmark for Federated Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13936)
*Daniel M. Jimenez-Gutierrez,Enrique Zuazua,Georgios Kellaris,Joaquin del Rio,Oleksii Sliusarenko,Xabi Uribe-Etxebarria*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种通过跨数据孤岛的联邦协作来解锁私有分布式机构数据以适应大型语言模型（LLM）的方法。基于Sherpa.ai联邦学习平台，该框架使各节点在不共享私有数据的前提下联合微调共享LLM。在医疗和金融领域的跨领域基准测试中，评估了三种参数高效微调（PEFT）策略（LoRA、QLoRA、IA3）在非独立同分布（non-IID）设置下的表现。结果表明，联邦微调性能接近集中式训练，优于单一机构孤立学习；从绿色AI角度，QLoRA和IA3在有限精度损失下提升效率，支持联邦PEFT作为无法共享数据场景下LLM适配的可行方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大型语言模型的发展依赖于公开数据集，但真正有价值的数据多为私有且分布在医疗、金融等受监管领域，因隐私、法规和组织壁垒无法共享。此外，这些数据通常呈现非独立同分布特征，导致传统方法难以有效利用。因此，亟需一种可在保护数据隐私前提下融合多方异构数据的新型协同学习范式。

Method: 基于Sherpa.ai联邦学习平台构建框架，实现跨机构节点间的联合微调，采用参数高效微调（PEFT）技术如LoRA、QLoRA、IA3，在不交换原始数据的情况下对共享大模型进行训练，并在医疗与金融领域的四个闭合式问答与分类任务上进行评估。

Result: 联邦微调在性能上接近集中式训练，显著优于单机构孤立学习；在非IID环境下仍保持良好泛化能力；QLoRA和IA3在降低计算资源消耗的同时仅带来轻微精度下降，展现出更高的能效比，验证了其在绿色AI背景下的可行性。

Conclusion: 本研究证明，通过联邦学习结合参数高效微调，可在不违反数据隐私与合规要求的前提下，有效利用分散的私有数据提升大模型的领域适应性。该方法为医疗、金融等领域的大模型落地提供了可扩展、可持续的技术路径。

Abstract: The recent success of large language models (LLMs) has been largely driven by vast public datasets. However, the next frontier for LLM development lies beyond public data. Much of the world's most valuable information is private, especially in highly regulated sectors such as healthcare and finance, where data include patient histories or customer communications. Unlocking this data could represent a major leap forward, enabling LLMs with deeper domain expertise and stronger real-world utility. Yet, these data cannot be shared because they are distributed across institutions and constrained by privacy, regulatory, and organizational barriers. Moreover, institutional datasets are typically non-independent and identically distributed (non-IID), differing across sites in population characteristics, data modalities, documentation patterns, and task-specific label distributions.
  In this paper, we demonstrate a practical approach to unlocking private and distributed institutional data for LLM adaptation through federated collaboration across data silos. Built on the Sherpa.ai Federated Learning platform, our framework enables nodes to jointly fine-tune a shared LLM without exchanging private data. We evaluate this approach through a cross-domain benchmark in healthcare and finance, using four closed-ended question answering and classification datasets: MedQA, MedMCQA, FPB, and FiQA-SA. We compare three parameter-efficient fine-tuning (PEFT) strategies-LoRA, QLoRA, and IA3-across pretrained backbones under non-IID settings reflecting institutional data heterogeneity. Our results show that federated fine-tuning performs close to centralized training and outperforms isolated single-institution learning. From a Green AI perspective, QLoRA and IA3 improve efficiency with limited accuracy degradation, supporting federated PEFT as a viable approach for adapting LLMs where data cannot be shared.

</details>


### [110] [EvolveMem:Self-Evolving Memory Architecture via AutoResearch for LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13941)
*Jiaqi Liu,Xinyu Ye,Peng Xia,Zeyu Zheng,Cihang Xie,Mingyu Ding,Huaxiu Yao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: EvolveMem 是一种自进化记忆架构，通过将检索配置作为结构化动作空间，由基于 LLM 的诊断模块进行优化。系统在每轮演化中分析失败日志，识别根本原因并提出针对性调整，结合自动回滚和探索停滞的保护机制，实现闭环自我进化。该过程无需人工干预，可自主发现有效检索策略，甚至拓展出原始动作空间之外的新维度。在 LoCoMo 和 MemBench 上均显著优于现有基线，且演化配置具备良好的跨基准迁移能力，表明其捕捉的是通用检索原则而非特定任务技巧。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆系统在长期运行中仅更新存储内容，而检索机制（如评分函数、融合策略、生成策略）固定不变，无法适应动态变化的需求。为实现真正自适应的记忆，需让知识与检索机制共同演化。

Method: 提出 EvolveMem 架构，将检索配置设为可优化的结构化动作空间；引入基于 LLM 的诊断模块，读取每问题失败日志，定位根因并生成配置调整建议；通过受控的元分析器实施调整，具备回滚和探索机制以保障稳定性。形成一个闭环的自研究（AutoResearch）流程。

Result: 在 LoCoMo 基准上，相对最强基线提升 25.7%，相比最小基线提升 78.0%；在 MemBench 上相对最强基线提升 18.9%。演化出的配置具有正向迁移能力，不产生灾难性遗忘，说明其学习到的是通用检索原理。

Conclusion: EvolveMem 实现了记忆系统的自进化，通过联合优化知识与检索机制，显著提升性能，并具备泛化能力。该方法为构建长期自主智能体提供了新范式。

Abstract: Long-term memory is essential for LLM agents that operate across multiple sessions, yet existing memory systems treat retrieval infrastructure as fixed: stored content evolves while scoring functions, fusion strategies, and answer-generation policies remain frozen at deployment. We argue that truly adaptive memory requires co-evolution at two levels: the stored knowledge and the retrieval mechanism that queries it. We present EvolveMem, a self-evolving memory architecture that exposes its full retrieval configuration as a structured action space optimized by an LLM-powered diagnosis module. In each evolution round, the module reads per-question failure logs, identifies root causes, and proposes targeted configuration adjustments; a guarded meta-analyzer applies them with automatic revert-on-regression and explore-on-stagnation safeguards. This closed-loop self-evolution realizes an AutoResearch process: the system autonomously conducts iterative research cycles on its own architecture, replacing manual configuration tuning. Starting from a minimal baseline, the process converges autonomously, discovering effective retrieval strategies including entirely new configuration dimensions not present in the original action space. On LoCoMo, EvolveMem outperforms the strongest baseline by 25.7% relative and achieves a 78.0% relative improvement over the minimal baseline. On MemBench, EvolveMem exceeds the strongest baseline by 18.9% relative. Evolved configurations transfer across benchmarks with positive rather than catastrophic transfer, indicating that the self-evolution process captures universal retrieval principles rather than benchmark-specific heuristics. Code is available at https://github.com/aiming-lab/SimpleMem.

### [111] [A Unified Geometric Framework for Weighted Contrastive Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13943)
*Raphael Vock,Edouard Duchesnay,Benoit Dufumier*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究将加权InfoNCE目标解释为距离几何问题，揭示了对比学习中嵌入几何结构的本质。研究表明，不同权重设计会影响嵌入的几何形态：在监督分类中，平衡数据下SupCon和Soft SupCon均生成规则单纯形结构，但类别不平衡时SupCon产生非均匀类间相似性，而Soft SupCon仍保持规则结构；在连续标签场景中，传统y-Aware CL因标签空间与潜在相似性空间不匹配而无法达到熵最优，而几何一致的权重设计（如欧氏-欧氏或X-CLR）可实现唯一最优嵌入。该框架为设计可实现、非退化且一致的对比学习目标提供了理论依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对比学习方法对嵌入空间几何结构的理解不足，导致其性能受数据分布和标签形式影响，缺乏系统性设计原则。本文旨在揭示权重设计如何决定嵌入几何的可实现性，从而建立统一的理论框架以指导对比学习目标的设计。

Method: 将加权InfoNCE目标建模为距离几何问题，通过数学分析推导不同权重策略下的最优嵌入结构，并结合几何约束验证其可实现性与一致性。

Result: 1. 监督分类中，平衡数据下所有方法生成规则单纯形；不平衡时，SupCon破坏对称性，Soft SupCon保持规则结构；2. 连续标签下，仅几何一致的权重（如欧氏-欧氏或X-CLR）能实现唯一最优嵌入，而标准y-Aware CL存在本质不匹配；3. 权重选择决定了对比学习是否可实现、退化或不一致。

Conclusion: 权重设计是决定对比学习嵌入几何性质的关键因素。本研究提出基于距离几何的统一视角，为构建几何可实现、稳定且鲁棒的对比学习目标提供了理论基础和设计准则。

Abstract: Contrastive learning (CL) aims to preserve relational structure between samples by learning representations that reflect a similarity graph. Yet, the geometry of the resulting embeddings remains poorly understood. Here we show that weighted InfoNCE objectives can be interpreted as Distance Geometry Problems, where the weighting scheme specifies the target geometry to be realized by the representation. This viewpoint yields exact characterizations of the optimal embeddings for several supervised and weakly supervised objectives. In supervised classification, both SupCon and Soft SupCon (a dense relaxation of it where pairs from distinct classes have small non-zero similarity) collapse samples within each class to a single prototype. However, while balanced SupCon recovers the classical regular simplex geometry, class imbalance breaks this symmetry: SupCon induces non-uniform inter-class similarities depending on class sizes, whereas Soft SupCon preserves a regular simplex geometry regardless of class imbalance. In continuous-label settings, our framework reveals a different failure mode: y-Aware CL generally cannot attain its entropic optimum unless the labels lie on a hypersphere, exposing a mismatch between Euclidean label weights and spherical latent similarity. By contrast, geometrically consistent choices such as Euclidean-Euclidean weighting or X-CLR admit unique optimal embeddings. Our results show that the choice of weighting scheme determines whether contrastive learning is geometrically realizable, degenerate, or inconsistent, providing a principled framework for designing contrastive objectives.

</details>

*Sinjae Kang,Chanyoung Kim,Kaixin Wang,Li Zhao,Kimin Lee*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前生成式机器人控制多采用标准高斯分布作为源分布，但其对时间动态建模能力有限，限制了策略性能。为提升控制精度与学习效率，需探索更具时序意义的先验分布。

Method: 提出温启先验（WarmPrior），利用最近的动作历史构造一个时间相关、平滑的先验分布，替换传统高斯源分布，并在扩散模型与流匹配框架下进行训练与评估。

Result: 在多种机器人操纵任务中，使用WarmPrior的模型显著提高成功率；概率路径更直，增强可解释性；在强化学习中，提升样本效率与最终性能。

Conclusion: 源分布是生成式机器人控制中一个关键且尚未充分探索的设计因素，引入时间感知的先验（如WarmPrior）可有效提升策略性能与学习效率。

Abstract: Generative policies based on diffusion and flow matching have become a dominant paradigm for visuomotor robotic control. We show that replacing the standard Gaussian source distribution with WarmPrior, a simple temporally grounded prior constructed from readily available recent action history, consistently improves success rates on robotic manipulation tasks. We trace this gain to markedly straighter probability paths, echoing the effect of optimal-transport couplings in Rectified Flow. Beyond standard behavior cloning, WarmPrior also reshapes the exploration distribution in prior-space reinforcement learning, improving both sample efficiency and final performance. Collectively, these results identify the source distribution as an important and underexplored design axis in generative robot control.

*Katherine Lambert,Sasha Luccioni*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种全面的能源核算框架，用于衡量知识蒸馏全流程的计算成本，通过分阶段追踪GPU功耗，揭示了传统方法中被忽略的教师模型侧能耗（如数据生成、logit缓存、评估等）。实验对比了两种常见蒸馏方法：基于logit的知识蒸馏与合成数据监督微调，构建了能源-质量帕累托前沿，并据此提出在能源和预算约束下的蒸馏方法与超参数选择准则。研究还开源了测量工具与核算协议，推动可重复、透明的蒸馏研究。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建分阶段的GPU功耗追踪系统，详细记录知识蒸馏各环节（如数据生成、日志缓存、评估、学生模型训练等）的能源消耗，实现端到端的能源会计。

Result: 发现教师侧工作负载占总能耗显著比例，传统评价方式低估了蒸馏的实际能源成本；通过构建能源-质量帕累托前沿，揭示不同蒸馏方法的能效权衡关系，提出优化设计规则。

Conclusion: 知识蒸馏并非总是节能高效的选择；必须考虑完整的管道能耗。本文提出的框架与工具为未来研究提供了标准化、可复现的能源问责基础。

Abstract: The rise in deployment of large language models has driven a surge in GPU demand and datacenter scaling, raising concerns about electricity use, grid stress, and the impacts of modern AI workloads. Distillation is often promoted as one of the most effective paths to obtain cheaper, more efficient models, yet these claims rarely account for the full end-to-end energy and resource costs, including crucial teacher-side workloads such as data generation, logit caching, and evaluation. We present a comprehensive energy accounting framework that measures the complete computational cost of distillation pipelines via detailed stage-wise tracking of GPU device power consumption. In our experiments, we separate and log empirical energy use across distinct phases and systematically measure the energy and emissions of two common distillation methods: the classic logit-based knowledge distillation and synthetic-data supervised fine-tuning, constructing energy-quality Pareto frontiers that expose the previously ignored costs. From these measurements and analyses, we derive practical design rules for selecting distillation methods and hyperparameters under energy and budget constraints, and release an open-source measurement harness and accounting protocol to provide a standardized foundation for comparable, reproducible distillation research, explicitly accountable for complete pipeline energy impact.

### [114] [TabPFN-3: Technical Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13986)
*Léo Grinsztajn,Klemens Flöge,Oscar Key,Felix Birkel,Philipp Jund,Brendan Roof,Mihir Manium,Shi Bin,Hoo,Magnus Bühler,Anurag Garg,Dominik Safaric,Jake Robertson,Benjamin Jäger,Simone Alessi,Adrian Hayler,Vladyslav Moroshan,Lennart Purucker,Philipp Singer,Alan Arazi,Julien Siems,Jan Hendrik Metzen,Georg Grab,Nick Erickson,Siyuan Guo,Eliott Kalfon,Simon Bing,David Salinas,Clara Cornu,Lilly Charlotte Wehrhahn,Diana Kriuchkova,Kursat Kaya,Lydia Sidhoum,Marie Salmon,Jerry Chen,Madelon Hulsebos,Yann LeCun,Samuel Müller,Bernhard Schölkopf,Sauraj Gambhir,Noah Hollmann,Frank Hutter*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TabPFN-3 是一个针对表格数据的前沿基础模型，可处理高达100万行的训练数据，显著提升预测性能并大幅降低训练与推理时间。它基于纯合成数据预训练，引入测试时计算扩展机制，并通过API（TabPFN-3-Plus）在多个基准上超越现有模型，包括在TabArena上超过其他模型200 Elo以上，且速度比AutoGluon快10倍。该模型在时间序列、关系型和表格-文本数据上均达到新SOTA水平，同时支持高效SHAP值计算（快120倍），且相比TabPFN-2.5最快达20倍加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前表格数据预测面临大规模数据下性能与效率难以兼顾的问题，现有模型在处理百万级样本时存在速度慢、资源消耗大等瓶颈。为突破这一限制，需发展更高效、可扩展的基础模型，以实现高性能与低延迟推理的统一。

Method: TabPFN-3采用基于合成数据的预训练策略，引入测试时计算扩展机制，结合减少的键值缓存与行块化处理技术，支持单张H100 GPU上处理100万行数据；其核心架构设计支持快速推理与大规模数据适配，并通过专门微调版本（如TabPFN-TS-3）拓展至时间序列与多模态任务。

Result: TabPFN-3在标准表格基准TabArena上表现卓越，单次前向传播即超越所有对比模型，且在速度与性能上实现帕累托最优。在多样化数据集上，其在高类别数场景排名第一，在百万级样本、200特征的数据上优于8小时调优的梯度提升树模型。其增强版TabPFN-3-Plus在TabArena上领先非TabPFN模型超200 Elo，最大子集达420 Elo，且比AutoGluon 1.5 extreme快10倍。此外，在RelBenchV1、TabSTAR等任务中达到新SOTA，SHAP计算加速达120倍，整体推理速度比前代快20倍。

Conclusion: TabPFN-3成功将表格基础模型推向新高度，实现了大规模数据下的高性能、低延迟预测，具备广泛的适用性与可扩展性，是当前表格数据建模领域的里程碑式进展。

Abstract: Tabular data underpins most high-value prediction problems in science and industry, and TabPFN has driven the foundation model revolution for this modality. Designed with feedback from our users, TabPFN-3 builds on this foundation to scale state-of-the-art performance to datasets with 1M training rows and substantially reduce training and inference time. Pretrained exclusively on synthetic data from our prior, TabPFN-3 dramatically pushes the frontier of tabular prediction and brings substantial gains on time series, relational, and tabular-text data. On the standard tabular benchmark TabArena, a forward pass of TabPFN-3 outperforms all other models, including tuned and ensembled baselines, by a significant margin, and pareto-dominates the speed/performance frontier. On more diverse datasets, TabPFN-3 ranks first on datasets with many classes, and beats 8-hour-tuned gradient-boosted-tree baselines on datasets up to 1M training rows and 200 features. TabPFN-3 introduces test-time compute scaling to tabular foundation models. Our API offering TabPFN-3-Plus (Thinking) exploits this to beat all non-TabPFN models by over 200 Elo on TabArena, rising to 420 Elo on the largest data subset, and outperforms AutoGluon 1.5 extreme while being 10x faster, without using LLMs, real data, internet search or any other model besides TabPFN. TabPFN-3 extends the capabilities of our models, enabling SOTA prediction on relational data (new SOTA foundation model on RelBenchV1) and tabular-text data (SOTA on TabSTAR via TabPFN-3-Plus); and improves existing integrations: a specialized checkpoint, TabPFN-TS-3, ranks 2nd on the time-series benchmark fev-bench, and SHAP-value computation is up to 120x faster. TabPFN-3 achieves this performance while being up to 20x faster than TabPFN-2.5. In addition, a reduced KV cache and row-chunking scale to 1M rows on one H100 with fast inference speed.

</details>


### [115] [HodgeCover: Higher-Order Topological Coverage Drives Compression of Sparse Mixture-of-Experts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13997)
*Tao Zhong,Dongzhe Zheng,Christine Allen-Blanchette*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出一种名为HodgeCover的新方法，用于学习-free的稀疏专家模型（MoE）压缩。其核心创新在于识别并利用专家间三元组合并的不可约循环障碍，通过霍奇分解（Hodge decomposition）提取2-复形上的调和核（harmonic kernel），从而精准定位关键的成对与三元合并障碍。HodgeCover通过贪婪覆盖调和关键边和三角形，在不重新训练的情况下实现高效压缩，优于现有基线，在极端压缩场景下表现更优，并在保留各霍奇分量质量方面具有独特平衡性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有学习-free MoE压缩方法受限于三元专家组合的不可约循环问题：两两兼容的专家合并后可能形成无法进一步合并的闭环结构，导致基于成对信号的压缩策略失效。因此需要一种能捕捉三元协同关系的新型压缩机制。

Method: 构建以专家为顶点、成对KL散度为边权重、三元组为面的2-复形；利用辛普利西尔拉普拉斯算子的调和核来刻画不可约三元组结构；通过霍奇分解分离出关键边与三角形，设计贪心算法HodgeCover进行覆盖选择，并结合传统权重剪枝形成混合压缩方案。

Result: 在三个开放权重的稀疏MoE模型上，HodgeCover在专家减少维度上达到当前最优水平，在混合压缩维度上领先于所有基线，且在四个霍奇分量中保持了最佳的质量分布平衡。

Conclusion: 揭示稀疏MoE结构中的调和核是理解其可压缩性的关键，这一发现使得新的压缩算法能在最具实际意义的高压缩率场景中胜出，标志着学习-free压缩进入新范式。

Abstract: Sparse Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) layers route tokens through a handful of experts, and learning-free compression of these layers reduces inference cost without retraining. A subtle obstruction blocks every existing compressor in this family: three experts can each be pairwise compatible yet form an irreducible cycle when merged together, so any score that ranks experts on pairwise signals is structurally blind to which triples are jointly mergeable. We show the obstruction is a precise mathematical object, the harmonic kernel of the simplicial Laplacian on a 2-complex whose vertices are experts, whose edges carry KL merge barriers, and whose faces carry triplet barriers; Hodge-decomposing the edge-barrier signal isolates the kernel exactly. We turn the diagnostic into a selection objective: HodgeCover greedily covers the harmonic-critical edges and triplet-critical triangles, and a hybrid variant of HodgeCover pairs it with off-the-shelf weight pruning on survivors. On three open-weight Sparse MoE backbones under aggressive expert reduction, HodgeCover matches state-of-the-art learning-free baselines on the expert-reduction axis, leads on the aggressive-compression frontier of the hybrid axis, and uniquely balances retained mass across all four Hodge components. These results show that exposing the harmonic kernel of a learned MoE structure changes which compressor wins at the regime that matters most.

</details>


### [116] [Support Before Frequency in Discrete Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13999)
*Adrian Müller,Antoine Gonon,Zebang Shen,Ya-Ping Hsieh,Niao He*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 离散扩散模型在语言建模中表现日益出色，但其去噪目标如何组织学习仍不清晰。本文揭示，在小噪声条件下，反向过程会形成粗粒度支持信息与细粒度频率信息的层级结构。均匀和吸收型扩散模型显示，单个词元的反向编辑可分解为决定是否趋向数据支持（如语法正确句子）的主导尺度，以及决定同一尺度内相对概率的精细系数。恢复有效性结构仅需学习反向概率的数量级，而恢复数据频率则需精确估计系数。不同机制导致不同行为：均匀扩散呈现三类编辑（改善、保持、恶化有效性），而吸收扩散则将主要质量集中在改善有效性的操作上。实验结果支持这些预测：支持定位先于支持内频率排序出现，且均匀与吸收扩散的速率差异符合预期。整体表明，离散扩散模型先学习数据支持，再学习数据频率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解离散扩散模型中去噪目标如何引导学习过程，特别是其对数据支持与频率信息的学习顺序和机制的影响。

Method: 理论分析结合实验验证：在小噪声极限下分析均匀和吸收型扩散模型的反向过程，推导出单个词元反向编辑的分解结构，并通过合成正则语言任务和掩码语言扩散模型实验检验预测。

Result: 支持局部化现象在训练早期出现，而支持内部频率排序较晚；均匀与吸收扩散模型表现出不同的编辑动态和学习速率，与理论预测一致。

Conclusion: 离散扩散模型优先学习数据支持，随后才精细学习数据频率，这一过程由扩散机制决定，具有明确的层次结构。

Abstract: Discrete diffusion models are increasingly competitive for language modeling, yet it remains unclear how their denoising objectives organize learning. Although these objectives target the full data distribution, we show that the exact reverse process induces a hierarchy between coarse support information and finer frequency information. For uniform and absorbing (a.k.a. masking) diffusion, we prove that, in the small-noise regime of the final denoising steps, each single-token reverse edit decomposes into a leading scale, determined by whether it moves toward the data support (e.g., grammatically valid sentences), and a finer coefficient, determining relative probabilities within the same scale. Thus, recovering validity structure only requires learning the correct order of magnitude of reverse probabilities, whereas recovering data frequencies requires coefficient-level estimation. The separation is mechanism-dependent: uniform diffusion exhibits a trichotomy into validity-improving, validity-preserving, and validity-worsening edits, while absorbing diffusion places its leading-order mass on validity-improving moves. Experiments on a masked language diffusion model and synthetic regular-language tasks support these predictions: support-localization emerges earlier than within-support frequency ranking, and the contrast between uniform and absorbing diffusion matches the predicted rate separation. Together, our results suggest that discrete diffusion models learn data support before data frequencies.

</details>


### [117] [Dywave: Event-Aligned Dynamic Tokenization for Heterogeneous IoT Sensing Signal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14014)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准分词技术难以应对物联网传感信号固有的非平稳性和多尺度特性，亟需一种能捕捉内在时间结构与物理事件的自适应分词方法。

Method: 采用小波基分层分解识别语义事件对应的时间边界，结合自适应压缩策略，在保留时间连贯性的前提下生成紧凑的输入表示。

Result: 在多个真实数据集上，Dywave 在准确率上最高提升12%，输入标记长度减少达75%，并表现出更强的鲁棒性与计算效率。

Conclusion: Dywave 有效解决了物联网传感信号动态分词难题，为智能应用提供了高效、鲁棒的序列建模基础。

Abstract: Internet of Things (IoT) systems continuously collect heterogeneous sensing signals from ubiquitous sensors to support intelligent applications such as human activity analysis, emotion monitoring, and environmental perception. These signals are inherently non-stationary and multi-scale, posing unique challenges for standard tokenization techniques. This paper proposes Dywave, a dynamic tokenization framework for IoT sensing signals that constructs compact input representations aligned with intrinsic temporal structures and underlying physical events. Dywave leverages wavelet-based hierarchical decomposition, identifies meaningful temporal boundaries corresponding to underlying semantic events, and adaptively compresses redundant intervals while preserving temporal coherence. Extensive evaluations on five real-world IoT sensing datasets across activity recognition, stress assessment, and nearby object detection demonstrate that Dywave outperforms state-of-the-art methods by up to 12% in accuracy, while improving computational efficiency by reducing input token lengths by up to 75% across mainstream sequence models. Moreover, Dywave exhibits improved robustness to domain shifts and varying sequence lengths.

### [118] [R2R2: Robust Representation for Intensive Experience Reuse via Redundancy Reduction in Self-Predictive Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14026)
*Sanghyeob Song,Donghyeok Lee,Jinsik Kim,Sungroh Yoon*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在数据稀缺领域（如真实机器人），高更新-数据比（UTD）虽提升效率但引发过拟合；现有工作多关注评论家偏差，而忽视了SPL中表示层面的不稳定性，亟需新方法解决此问题。

Method: 提出R2R2正则化方法，基于对SPL谱特性的理论分析，摒弃传统零中心化，采用非中心化目标以减少冗余，提升表示稳定性；应用于TD7，并扩展至SimbaV2-SPL框架。

Result: 在11个连续控制任务上验证，R2R2有效缓解过拟合；在UTD=20时，使TD7性能提升约22%；在SimbaV2-SPL基础上仍带来额外增益，实现新的最优性能。

Conclusion: R2R2通过减少表示冗余，有效提升了SPL在高UTD下的稳定性与泛化能力，为数据稀缺环境下的强化学习提供了高效且鲁棒的新解决方案。

Abstract: For reinforcement learning in data-scarce domains like real-world robotics, intensive data reuse enhances efficiency but induces overfitting. While prior works focus on critic bias, representation-level instability in Self-Predictive Learning (SPL) under high Update-to-Data (UTD) regimes remains underexplored. To bridge this gap, we propose Robust Representation via Redundancy Reduction (R2R2), a regularization method within SPL. We theoretically identify that standard zero-centering conflicts with SPL's spectral properties and design a non-centered objective accordingly. We verify R2R2 on SPL-native algorithms like TD7. Furthermore, to demonstrate its orthogonality to prior advancements, we extend the state-of-the-art SimbaV2, which originally lacks SPL, by integrating a tailored SPL module, termed SimbaV2-SPL. Experiments across 11 continuous control tasks confirm that R2R2 effectively mitigates overfitting; specifically, at a UTD ratio of 20, it improves TD7 by ~22% and provides additional gains on top of SimbaV2-SPL, which itself establishes a new state-of-the-art. The code can be found at: https://github.com/songsang7/R2R2

### [119] [Self-Pruned Key-Value Attention: Learning When to Write by Predicting Future Utility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14037)
*Gergely Szilvasy,Manuel Faysse,Maria Lomeli,Matthijs Douze,Pierre-Emmanuel Mazaré,Loïc Cabannes,Wen-tau Yih,Hervé Jégou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出Self-Pruned Key-Value Attention（SP-KV）机制，通过轻量级预测器动态评估每个键值对的未来使用价值，仅缓存高价值的旧键值对，实现KV缓存的动态稀疏化，显著降低内存占用和带宽压力，提升生成效率，同时保持模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在现代测试时计算和智能体范式下，语言模型处理序列长度不断增加，导致Transformer架构中的键值（KV）缓存内存占用和带宽成为瓶颈，亟需高效压缩策略以支持长序列生成。

Method: 引入轻量级实用度预测器，对每个键值对进行细粒度评分；近期键值对始终保留在局部窗口中，而较早的键值对仅当其预测实用度超过阈值时才被写入缓存并用于全局注意力；整个模型与预测器通过端到端的下一词预测损失联合训练，从预训练检查点中微调。

Result: 实现了3至10倍的KV缓存压缩率，显著提升内存效率与解码速度，验证损失和下游任务性能几乎无下降；揭示出分层与头级别的结构化稀疏模式，可指导混合局部-全局注意力架构的设计。

Conclusion: SP-KV是一种高效的动态稀疏化机制，能够自适应地减少长期KV缓存规模，在不牺牲性能的前提下大幅提升长序列生成的效率，同时为注意力架构设计提供新思路。

Abstract: Under modern test-time compute and agentic paradigms, language models process ever-longer sequences. Efficient text generation with transformer architectures is increasingly constrained by the Key-Value cache memory footprint and bandwidth. To address this limitation, we introduce Self-Pruned Key-Value Attention (SP-KV), a mechanism designed to predict future KV utility in order to reduce the size of the long-term KV cache. This strategy operates at a fine granularity: a lightweight utility predictor scores each key-value pair, and while recent KVs are always available via a local window, older pairs are written in the cache and used in global attention only if their predicted utility surpasses a given threshold. The LLM and the utility predictor are trained jointly end-to-end exclusively through next-token prediction loss, and are adapted from pretrained LLM checkpoints.
  Rather than enforcing a fixed compression ratio, SP-KV performs dynamic sparsification: the mechanism adapts to the input and typically reduces the KV cache size by a factor of $3$ to $10\times$, longer sequences often being more compressible. This leads to vast improvements in memory usage and decoding speed, with little to no degradation of validation loss nor performance on a broad set of downstream tasks. Beyond serving as an effective KV-cache reduction mechanism, our method reveals structured layer- and head-specific sparsity patterns that we can use to guide the design of hybrid local-global attention architectures.

### [120] [Reliability-Gated Source Anchoring for Continual Test-Time Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14063)
*Vikash Singh,Debargha Ganguly,Weicong Chen,Sabyasachi Sahoo,Sreehari Sankar,Biyao Zhang,Mohsen Harir,Shouren Wang,Osama Zafar,Christian Gagné,Vipin Chaudhary*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: RMemSafe 是一种可靠性门控的持续测试时自适应方法，通过冻结源模型的归一化预测熵来动态调节源锚定强度。当源模型可靠性下降（熵接近均匀分布）时，系统自动关闭源锚定和一致性过滤，转而采用无源基线损失与边缘校准，实现更稳健的性能。在9个连续退化场景中表现优异，显著优于现有方法，尤其在源模型严重退化时展现出更平缓的性能衰减，有效避免了传统方法中的‘盲锚定’问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有源锚定的持续测试时自适应方法在源模型可靠性下降时仍保持固定锚定强度，导致性能急剧恶化，这种现象称为‘盲锚定’。尤其在复杂退化数据集CCC-Hard上，源模型准确率降至1.3%，但传统方法未察觉并继续使用无效锚点，造成严重性能损失。因此需要一种能感知源模型可靠性并自适应调整的机制。

Method: 提出RMemSafe，基于ROID框架扩展，引入一个由源模型预测熵控制的可靠性门控机制。该门控用于衰减所有显式依赖源模型的项（如源锚定、一致性过滤）。当源预测熵接近均匀分布（即源不可靠）时，门控关闭，源相关项消失，模型退化为仅包含基础损失和边缘校准的无源鲁棒目标。

Result: RMemSafe在8/9个匹配分割的持续退化任务中达到最低误差，在全部9个任务中作为基于重置的方法表现最佳。相较于ROID+ASR，ResNet-50提升1.05个百分点，ViT-B/16提升0.48个百分点。在源模型逐步退化实验中，性能下降斜率比ROID+ASR低1.13倍，验证了其优雅降级特性。门控机制能准确识别高熵源崩溃，而非误判低熵但错误的源。

Conclusion: RMemSafe通过引入可靠性门控机制，有效解决了持续测试时自适应中的‘盲锚定’问题，实现了在源模型失效时的稳健过渡。该方法不仅提升了模型在极端退化条件下的鲁棒性，还提供了可解释的可靠性判断依据，为未来持续学习系统的设计提供了新思路。

Abstract: Continual test-time adaptation (CTTA) updates a pretrained model online on an unlabeled, non-stationary stream while anchoring it to a frozen source checkpoint. This anchor is useful only when the source remains reliable. On CCC-Hard, however, a ResNet-50 source falls to approximately $1.3\%$ top-$1$ accuracy, while existing source-anchored CTTA methods continue applying the same anchor strength. We call this failure mode blind anchoring and propose RMemSafe, a reliability-gated extension of ROID that uses the frozen source's normalized predictive entropy to attenuate all explicit source-coupled uses in the objective. When the source posterior approaches uniformity, the gate closes: the source anchor and agreement filter vanish, and the objective reduces to a source-agnostic fallback comprising ROID's base losses plus marginal calibration. Combined with ASR, RMemSafe achieves the lowest error on $8$ of $9$ matched-split continual-corruption cells and is the best reset-based method on all $9$, improving ROID+ASR by $1.05$~pp on ResNet-50 and $0.48$~pp on ViT-B/16. A controlled source-degradation sweep shows a $1.13{\times}$ shallower harm slope than ROID+ASR, consistent with the graceful-decay prediction. The entropy gate detects high-entropy source collapse, not confidently wrong low-entropy sources; this scope is explicitly evaluated and discussed.

### [121] [AttnGen: Attention-Guided Saliency Learning for Interpretable Genomic Sequence Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14073)
*Rayhaneh Shabani Nia,Ali Karkehabadi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: AttnGen is an attention-guided training framework that enhances interpretability in genomic sequence classification by using attention to compute nucleotide-level importance scores and suppressing low-contribution positions during training. It improves accuracy (96.73% vs. 95.83% for CNN), accelerates convergence, and boosts stability. Perturbation analysis confirms that the model relies on a small subset of high-saliency positions. Masking 10–20% of positions optimally balances performance and interpretability.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing deep neural networks in genomics lack interpretability; understanding which sequence elements drive predictions is crucial for biological insight. This work aims to embed interpretability directly into the model's training process.

Method: AttnGen uses an attention mechanism to assign importance scores to nucleotides and progressively masks low-importance positions during training, guiding the model to focus on informative regions.

Result: AttnGen achieves higher validation accuracy (96.73%) than a CNN baseline (95.83%), converges faster, and shows greater training stability. Removing high-saliency nucleotides reduces accuracy to near chance level, confirming reliance on a compact set of key positions. Optimal performance-interpretability trade-off occurs with 10–20% masking.

Conclusion: Attention-guided masking improves both predictive performance and interpretability in genomic sequence modeling. The approach is promising for interpretable learning in genomics and may extend to more complex sequence tasks.

Abstract: Deep neural networks have achieved strong performance in genomic sequence classification; however, relating their predictions to biologically meaningful sequence patterns remains challenging. In this work, we present AttnGen, an attention-guided training framework that embeds interpretability directly into the optimization process. AttnGen computes nucleotide-level importance scores using an attention mechanism and progressively suppresses low-contribution positions during training. This encourages the model to focus its predictions on a compact set of informative regions while reducing reliance on noisy sequence elements. We evaluate AttnGen on the standardized demo_human_or_worm benchmark, a binary classification task over 200-nucleotide sequences. With moderate masking, AttnGen achieves a validation accuracy of 96.73%, outperforming a conventional CNN baseline with 95.83% accuracy, while also exhibiting faster convergence and improved training stability. To assess whether the learned importance scores reflect functionally relevant signal, we conduct perturbation-based analysis by removing high-saliency nucleotides. This causes accuracy to drop from 96.9% to near chance level on a 3,000-sequence evaluation set, indicating that the model relies on a relatively small subset of informative positions. Our analysis shows that masking 10--20% of positions provides the most favorable trade-off between predictive performance and interpretability. These results suggest that attention-guided masking not only improves classification performance but also reshapes how models distribute importance across sequence positions. Although this study focuses on short genomic sequences, the proposed approach may extend to more complex interpretable sequence modeling settings.

### [122] [Fair and Calibrated Toxicity Detection with Robust Training and Abstention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14074)
*Mokshit Surana*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了毒性分类中的公平性问题，涵盖排序、校准和回避三个维度。通过对比ERM、实例级重加权和Group DRO，并结合温度缩放、基于置信度的回避及按身份优化阈值等后处理方法，发现训练阶段的干预直接影响后处理效果。主要发现包括：校准偏差是隐藏的不公平现象；训练干预虽改善排序但加剧校准差距或导致全局均匀偏差；后处理方法继承训练缺陷；回避机制本身也存在不公平。强调需采用多轴框架评估SRAI公平性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在训练和后处理阶段独立评估，忽视了二者之间的相互影响。实际应用中，模型在不同身份子群体上的表现差异可能导致严重社会后果，因此需要系统性地从多个公平性维度综合评估模型行为。

Method: 比较Empirical Risk Minimization (ERM)、实例级重加权和Group DRO三种训练策略，结合温度缩放、置信度回避和按身份调整阈值等后处理技术，在子群AUC、BPSN/BNSP AUC、误差差距和分组期望校准误差（ECE）等指标上进行评估，使用bootstrap置信区间（n=1000）分析统计显著性。

Result: （1）ERM虽整体校准良好（ECE=0.013），但在各身份子群中均存在显著校准偏差（+0.029至+0.134）；（2）重加权ERM提升排序性能但恶化校准公平性（最大增加0.232）；Group DRO消除子群校准差异，但导致整体均匀偏误（ECE=0.118）；（3）温度缩放因非均匀校准失效；基于置信度的回避在ERM下有效，但在DRO下导致风险-覆盖率曲线上升；（4）回避机制对背景内容更有利，对提及身份的内容不公平。

Conclusion: SRAI公平性必须采用多轴评估框架。仅关注聚合排名的方法可能掩盖深层失败模式，这些模式决定了真实世界中的伤害程度。训练与后处理应协同设计，避免将训练阶段的不公平转移至后续环节。

Abstract: Fairness in toxicity classification involves three integrated axes: ranking, calibration, and abstention. Training-time interventions and post-hoc safety mechanisms cannot be evaluated independently because the former determines the efficacy of the latter. We compare Empirical Risk Minimization (ERM), instance-level reweighting, and Group DRO across these axes, combined with temperature scaling, confidence-based abstention, and per-identity threshold optimization. Evaluation uses subgroup AUC, BPSN/BNSP AUC, error gaps, and per-subgroup Expected Calibration Error (ECE) with bootstrap CIs ($n = 1000$).
  We report four findings. (1) Calibration disparity is a hidden fairness violation. ERM has near-perfect aggregate calibration ($0.013$) but is significantly miscalibrated across all identity subgroups ($+0.029$ to $+0.134$). (2) Training interventions reshape rather than eliminate disparity. Reweighted ERM improves ranking (BPSN AUC $+0.06$ to $+0.12$) but worsens the calibration-fairness gap by up to $+0.232$. Group DRO eliminates calibration disparity but only by becoming uniformly miscalibrated globally (ECE $0.118$). (3) Post-hoc methods inherit training failure modes. Temperature scaling fails because miscalibration is non-uniform. Confidence-based abstention works under ERM but breaks under DRO, where the risk-coverage curve rises with deferral. (4) Abstention itself is unfair. Confidence-based deferral helps background content far more than identity-mentioning content. We argue that SRAI fairness requires a multi-axis framework: methods that differ only in aggregate ranking can differ sharply in failure modes that determine real-world harm.

Result: 实现了在回归和分类任务中对不确定性的有效量化，显著提升了训练效率和模型性能，且具备良好的用户友好性与易用性。

Conclusion: bde 为表格数据上的贝叶斯深度集成提供了高效、可扩展且易用的解决方案，适用于需要不确定性建模的实际场景。

Abstract: bde is a user-friendly Python package for Bayesian Deep Ensembles with a particular focus on tabular data. Built on an efficient JAX implementation of the sampling-based inference method Microcanonical Langevin Ensembles (MILE), it provides scikit-learn compatible estimators for fast training, efficient Markov Chain Monte Carlo sampling, and uncertainty quantification in both regression and classification tasks.

### [124] [Uncovering Trajectory and Topological Signatures in Multimodal Pediatric Sleep Embeddings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14156)
*Scott Ye,Harlin Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了多模态掩码自编码器生成的30秒儿科多导睡眠图（PSG）片段嵌入序列中的会话级诊断信息，通过引入PHATE衍生的每段坐标、整晚运动特征、嵌入云的持久同调总结以及电子健康记录（EHR），验证了这些特征在任务中的相关性。采用简单线性与MLP模型以确保可解释性，结果表明几何、拓扑和临床特征均提供互补增益。在二分类任务中，特征重要性因任务而异，更复杂的后期融合模型表现更优，AUPRC显著提升：低氧饱和度从0.26升至0.34，脑电觉醒从0.31升至0.48，低通气从0.09升至0.22，呼吸暂停从0.05升至0.14。同时，全融合模型在Brier得分和预期校准误差上表现最佳，说明其在极端不平衡下的校准性能更优。研究揭示了潜在几何/拓扑结构与EHR数据能提供超越嵌入本身、具有可解释性的补充信号，提升模型鲁棒性与可靠性。

We test whether augmenting embeddings with PHATE-derived per-epoch coordinates and whole-night movement descriptors, persistent homology summaries of the embedding cloud, and EHR yields task-relevant signals. Method: 采用非渐近分析方法，结合分数匹配技术，推导出学习多项式形式指数族结构时所需的样本复杂度边界。

### [126] [LLMs Know When They Know, but Do Not Act on It: A Metacognitive Harness for Test-time Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14186)
*Qi Cao,Yufan Wang,Peijia Qin,Shuhao Zhang,Pengtao Xie*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种元认知引导机制，通过分离监控与推理过程，利用大语言模型在解题前的‘知觉感’（FOK）和解题后的‘学习判断’（JOL）信号，实现测试时的推理控制。该机制决定何时信任当前答案、何时基于元认知反馈重试，或何时将多次尝试结果交由聚合器处理。在文本、代码和多模态推理基准上，该方法显著提升了固定Claude Sonnet-4.6模型的性能，准确率从48.3提升至56.9，并超越多个主流基准的领先榜单表现，表明强语言模型具备潜在的元认知能力，但需通过显式控制框架加以利用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型虽能自我评估成功可能性与答案正确性，但这些信号通常仅用于测量而非控制推理过程。本文旨在探索是否可将此类元认知信号转化为有效的测试时控制机制，以提升模型推理表现。

Method: 受认知心理学中Nelson-Narens理论启发，提出一种元认知引导框架：先让模型输出解题前的‘知觉感’（FOK），再在每次解题后输出‘学习判断’（JOL）；基于这两个信号构建控制逻辑，决定是否接受当前解、是否重试并注入元认知反馈，或是否将多轮尝试结果交由聚合器处理。

Result: 在多个公开基准测试中，该方法在不进行参数更新或微调的情况下，将固定模型的综合准确率从48.3提升至56.9，并在HLE-Verified、LiveCodeBench v6和R-Bench-V三个主要评测设置上超过现有最强榜单成绩。

Conclusion: 强大的大语言模型已具备潜在的元认知能力，但需要通过显式的控制框架才能在推理过程中有效运用。本研究证明了元认知信号可通过结构化控制机制显著提升模型性能。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) often expose useful signals of self-monitoring: before solving a problem, they can estimate whether they are likely to succeed, and after solving it, they can judge whether their answer is likely to be correct. However, these signals are typically measured or elicited in isolation, rather than used to control inference. In this work, we ask whether LLMs possess latent metacognitive ability that can be turned into effective test-time control. Inspired by the Nelson--Narens theory from cognitive psychology, we propose a metacognitive harness that separates monitoring from reasoning. For each problem, the model first reports a pre-solve feeling-of-knowing (FOK) signal; after each solve attempt, it reports a post-solve judgment-of-learning (JOL) signal. Rather than treating these signals as passive confidence estimates, the harness turns them into an explicit control interface for reasoning: it decides when to trust the current solution, when to retry with compact metacognitive feedback, and when to pass multiple attempts to a final aggregator. Across text, code, and multimodal reasoning benchmarks, our harness substantially improves a fixed Claude Sonnet-4.6 base model without parameter updates or benchmark-specific fine-tuning. On the evaluated public benchmark snapshots, it raises pooled accuracy from 48.3 to 56.9 and exceeds the strongest listed leaderboard entries on the three primary evaluation settings: HLE-Verified, LiveCodeBench v6, and R-Bench-V. These results suggest that strong LLMs may already possess useful metacognitive ability, but require an explicit control harness to act on it during reasoning.

### [128] [PreFT: Prefill-only finetuning for efficient inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14217)
*Andrew Lanpouthakoun,Aryaman Arora,Zhengxuan Wu,Dhruv Pai,Ben Keigwin,Dan Jurafsky,Christopher Potts*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出PreFT（Prefill-only Finetuning），仅在预填充阶段应用适配器，生成阶段丢弃适配器，以提升多适配器服务的吞吐量。该方法在保持性能的同时显著提高效率，在Llama 3.1 70B上实现512个适配器时吞吐量提升1.9倍。实验表明，尽管在监督微调任务中评估损失略高，但通过增加秩可有效补偿；在强化学习任务中，PreFT与传统PEFT表现接近。整体验证了PreFT在个性化推理中更优的准确率-吞吐量权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有参数高效微调方法（PEFT）在多用户个性化服务中因预填充与解码阶段的性能不匹配导致吞吐量下降，尤其在解码阶段多个适配器并行时问题严重。因此需要从优化参数数量转向优化服务吞吐量。

Method: 提出PreFT方法，仅在预填充阶段使用适配器，解码阶段移除适配器，减少内存和计算开销。实现并发布基于vLLM引擎的LoRA和ReFT两种预填充仅适配方案。

Result: 在Llama 3.1 70B上，512个适配器并发时，PreFT比传统PEFT提升1.9倍吞吐量；监督微调任务中损失略高但可通过增加秩补偿；强化学习任务中表现接近标准PEFT。

Conclusion: PreFT为个性化大模型服务提供了更优的准确率-吞吐量平衡，是面向大规模多用户场景下更高效的微调部署策略。

Abstract: Large language models can now be personalised efficiently at scale using parameter efficient finetuning methods (PEFTs), but serving user-specific PEFTs harms throughput, even with specialised kernels and memory management techniques. This is because, theoretically and empirically, a mismatch exists between prefill (processing a large number of tokens at once) and decode (generating a single token autoregressively): the latter has far lower throughput when serving multiple adapters. Rather than optimising performance relative to parameter count, for efficient multi-adapter serving, we instead ought to optimise performance relative to serving throughput. We therefore propose PreFT (Prefill-only Finetuning), wherein we only apply the adapter to prefill tokens and discard it afterwards. PreFT significantly increases throughput with minimal effect on performance. We develop and release an efficient implementation of two prefill-only PEFTs, LoRA and ReFT, on the vLLM inference engine. We first show that serving multi-user PreFTs is more efficient than traditional PEFTs ($1.9\times$ the throughput when serving $512$ adapters on Llama 3.1 70B). Then, we compare the performance of prefill-only vs. all-token adapters on a variety of supervised finetuning and reinforcement learning tasks with LMs at varying scales. On SFT, we observe that the evaluation loss of PreFTs is higher than PEFTs, but can be compensated by increasing rank with nearly no reduction in throughput. On RL, we consistently find that PreFTs approach parity with standard PEFTs. Together, this work validates prefill-only adaptation of LLMs as a more favourable accuracy-throughput tradeoff than existing PEFTs for personalised serving.

</details>


### [129] [Diagnosing Training Inference Mismatch in LLM Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14220)
*Tianle Zhong,Neiwen Ling,Yifan Pi,Zijun Wei,Tianshu Yu,Geoffrey Fox,Peng Wu,Xiao Yu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出在零错配诊断设置（VeXact）中隔离训练-推理不匹配（TIM），发现微小的令牌级数值差异可独立导致训练崩溃，并揭示TIM改变了有效优化问题，提出一系列缓解措施。研究强调TIM并非无害的数值噪声，而是一种应作为系统级扰动首要考虑的因素，影响大模型强化学习的稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大模型强化学习系统在滚动生成与策略优化阶段存在实现差异，导致相同序列在相同模型权重下产生不同的词元概率，引发训练-推理不匹配（TIM）。这种不匹配难以检测，因与非策略漂移和稳定机制交织在一起。因此需要一种方法来分离并分析TIM的本质影响。

Method: 构建零错配诊断环境VeXact，隔离出TIM效应；通过控制实验验证不同数值差异对训练过程的影响；分析TIM如何改变优化目标，并评估多种缓解方案的有效性。

Result: 发现即使微小的令牌级数值差异也能独立引发训练崩溃；TIM显著改变有效优化问题；提出的若干修复措施能有效缓解该问题；证实TIM是系统级扰动而非简单噪声。

Conclusion: TIM不是可忽略的数值偏差，而是影响大模型强化学习系统稳定性的关键因素，必须在系统设计和训练分析中优先考虑。

Abstract: Modern LLM RL systems separate rollout generation from policy optimization. These two stages are expected to produce token probabilities that match exactly. However, implementation differences can make them assign different values to the same sequence under the same model weights, inducing Training-Inference Mismatch (TIM). TIM is difficult to inspect because it is entangled with off-policy drift and common stabilization mechanisms. In this work, we isolate TIM in a zero-mismatch diagnostic setting (VeXact), and show that small token-level numerical disagreements can independently cause training collapse. We further show that TIM changes the effective optimization problem, and identify a set of remedies that could mitigate TIM. Our results suggest that TIM is not benign numerical noise, but a systems-level perturbation that should be treated as a first-order factor in analyzing LLM RL stability.

While recent advances have been driven mainly by generative reconstruction objectives, contrastive approaches remain less explored, partly due to the difficulty of designing effective audio augmentations and the large batch sizes required for contrastive pre-training. We introduce \textbf{AudioMosaic}, a contrastive learning-based audio encoder for general audio understanding. During pre-training, AudioMosaic constructs positive pairs by applying structured time-frequency masking to spectrogram patches, which reduces memory usage and enables efficient large-batch training. Compared with generative approaches, the AudioMosaic encoder learns more discriminative utterance-level representations that demonstrate strong transferability across datasets, domains, and acoustic conditions. Extensive experiments show that AudioMosaic achieves state-of-the-art performance on several standard audio benchmarks under both linear probing and fine-tuning. We further show that integrating the pretrained AudioMosaic encoder into audio-language models improves performance on audio-language tasks. The code is publicly available in our \href{https://github.com/HanxunH/AudioMosaic}{GitHub repository}.

### [131] [Active Learners as Efficient PRP Rerankers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14236)
*Jeremías Figueiredo Paschmann,Juan Kaplan,Francisco Nattero Santiago Mauricio Barron Bucolo,Juan Wisznia,Luciano del Corro*

TL;DR: Pairwise Ranking Prompting (PRP) uses LLMs to generate pairwise preferences, but noise and intransitivity undermine traditional sorting. This paper reframes PRP as active learning, proposing a noise-robust framework with a randomized-direction oracle that reduces cost by using one LLM call per pair while eliminating position bias.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional sorting assumptions fail in noisy, order-sensitive, and intransitive pairwise judgment settings. Truncating full permutations for budget constraints leads to unreliable top-K rankings.

Method: Reframe PRP as active learning from noisy comparisons; introduce a randomized-direction oracle that uses one LLM call per pair, converting systematic position bias into zero-mean noise for unbiased aggregation.

Result: Active rankers outperform traditional sorting in NDCG@10 per call under call constraints. The randomized-direction oracle achieves better ranking quality with lower cost and improved robustness to noise.

Conclusion: By modeling PRP as active learning and introducing a noise-robust, single-call oracle, the proposed framework significantly improves ranking reliability and efficiency in constrained LLM evaluation scenarios.

Abstract: Pairwise Ranking Prompting (PRP) elicits pairwise preference judgments from an LLM, which are then aggregated into a ranking, usually via classical sorting algorithms. However, judgments are noisy, order-sensitive, and sometimes intransitive, so sorting assumptions do not match the setting. Because sorting aims to recover a full permutation, truncating it to meet a call budget does not produce a dependable top-K. We thus reframe PRP reranking as active learning from noisy pairwise comparisons and show that active rankers are drop-in replacements that improve NDCG@10 per call in the call-constrained regime. Our noise-robust framework also introduces a randomized-direction oracle that uses a single LLM call per pair. This approach converts systematic position bias into zero-mean noise, enabling unbiased aggregate ranking without the cost of bidirectional calls.

### [133] [Latency-Quality Routing for Functionally Equivalent Tools in LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14241)
*Kexin Chu,Dawei Xiang,Wei Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: LQM-ContextRoute 是一种基于上下文的强化学习路由算法，用于在多个功能等价的工具提供者之间进行高效选择。它通过将延迟与回答质量匹配，以每服务周期的预期回答质量为排序依据，结合查询特定的质量估计和 LLM 作为裁判的反馈，实现在线自适应。该方法在不同负载和提供者异质性条件下均表现优异，在 Web 搜索、策略问答和检索器池等任务中显著优于 SW-UCB 基线，提升准确率和排序质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在实际部署中，相同功能的工具（如搜索接口、检索器、LLM 后端）存在多个提供者，它们在延迟、可靠性和答案质量上差异显著，且缺乏黄金标签。如何在运行时根据动态负载和性能差异智能选择最优提供者，成为关键挑战。传统方法常因延迟与质量的加性奖励设计导致性能下降，尤其在高异质性场景下失效。

Method: 提出 LQM-ContextRoute，一种基于上下文的多臂赌博机路由机制。核心是延迟-质量匹配：将延迟视为服务能力，以单位服务周期的预期答案质量为核心评分指标；融合查询相关的质量预测、容量感知评分以及 LLM 作为裁判的反馈信号，实现对负载变化和提供者差异的在线适应。

Result: 在主流 Web 搜索基准测试中，相比 SW-UCB，F1 提升 +2.18 个百分点，同时保持在延迟-质量前沿；在高异质性的 StrategyQA 场景中，避免了加性奖励崩溃问题，准确率最高提升 +18 个百分点；在异构检索器池中，NDCG 提升 +2.91 至 +3.22 个百分点。结果表明，将延迟视为服务容量能有效提升路由性能，尤其是在高负载和异质性共存时。

Conclusion: LQM-ContextRoute 证明了在同功能工具路由中，将延迟视为服务容量并据此优化质量效率的重要性。该方法能够有效应对真实部署中的动态负载和提供者异质性，显著提升系统整体性能，具备良好的实用价值。

Abstract: Tool-augmented LLM agents increasingly access the same tool type through multiple functionally equivalent providers, such as web-search APIs, retrievers, or LLM backends exposed behind a shared interface. This creates a provider-routing problem under runtime load: the router must choose among providers that differ in latency, reliability, and answer quality, often without gold labels at deployment time. We introduce LQM-ContextRoute, a contextual bandit router for same-function tool providers. Its key design is latency-quality matching: instead of letting low latency offset poor answers in an additive reward, the router ranks providers by expected answer quality per service cycle. It combines this capacity-aware score with query-specific quality estimation and LLM-as-judge feedback, allowing it to adapt online to both load changes and provider-quality differences. On the main web-search load benchmark, LQM-ContextRoute improves F1 by +2.18 pp over SW-UCB while staying on the latency-quality frontier. In a high-heterogeneity StrategyQA setting, LQM-ContextRoute avoids additive-reward collapse and improves accuracy by up to +18 pp over SW-UCB; on heterogeneous retriever pools, it improves NDCG by +2.91--+3.22 pp over SW-UCB. These results show that same-function tool routing benefits from treating latency as service capacity, especially when runtime pressure and provider-quality heterogeneity coexist.

### [135] [Architecture-Aware Explanation Auditing for Industrial Visual Inspection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14255)
*Sibo Jia,Zihang Zhao,Kunrong Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于原生读出假设的架构感知解释审计协议，揭示了深度模型解释方法的可信度受其结构与模型原生决策机制距离的影响。在WM-811K晶圆图数据集上，ViT-Tiny+Attention Rollout虽分类准确率较低，但删除法AUC仅为0.211，显著低于Swin-Tiny、ResNet18+CBAM等模型搭配Grad-CAM的表现（0.432–0.525），且效应量绝对值超过1.1。研究发现，决定解释可信度的关键是读出结构而非模型架构家族；例如Swin-Tiny虽为Transformer，但其空间特征层次使其兼容Grad-CAM。模型无关方法RISE的性能普遍低于本地方法，表明原生读出并非最优，而是兼容性原则。不同扰动基线（如模糊填充）会导致解释可信度排序反转，说明评估结果依赖于（模型, 解释器, 扰动算子）三元组。在MVTec AD上的探索性研究进一步表明，审计结果具有任务和数据集依赖性。最终建议：解释路径应与模型架构协同设计，并在部署时提供量化可信度指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前工业视觉检测系统依赖深度分类器，其热力图解释虽外观合理，却可能无法准确反映真正驱动决策的图像区域，亟需可信赖的解释评估方法。现有方法缺乏对解释路径与模型架构之间关系的系统性理解，尤其忽视了读出结构对解释可信度的影响。

Method: 提出架构感知解释审计协议，基于原生读出假设，通过零填充扰动（three-seed zero-fill perturbation）评估多种模型（ViT-Tiny, Swin-Tiny, ResNet18+CBAM, DenseNet121）与解释方法（Attention Rollout, Grad-CAM, RISE）组合的删除法AUC。引入对比分析、扰动基线敏感性测试及边界条件研究，系统检验解释可信度的决定因素。

Result: ViT-Tiny+Attention Rollout在删除法下表现最差（AUC=0.211），而其他模型搭配对应解释方法表现更优（AUC=0.432–0.525）。Swin-Tiny显示读出结构比架构家族更具决定性。模型无关方法RISE整体表现低于本地方法，但优于部分原生方法，说明原生读出是兼容性而非最优性保障。不同扰动基线导致可信度排序反转，证实评估结果依赖三元组。边界研究揭示结果具有数据集与任务依赖性。

Conclusion: 解释方法的可信度不仅取决于模型架构，更关键的是其与模型原生读出结构的匹配程度。应将解释路径与模型架构协同设计，并在部署中加入定量可信度评估，以提升工业视觉系统的可解释性与可靠性。

Abstract: Industrial visual inspection systems increasingly rely on deep classifiers whose heatmap explanations may appear visually plausible while failing to identify the image regions that actually drive model decisions. This paper operationalizes an architecture-aware explanation audit protocol grounded in the native-readout hypothesis: the perturbation-based faithfulness of an explanation method is bounded by its structural distance from the model's native decision mechanism. On WM-811K wafer maps (9 classes, 172k images) under a three-seed zero-fill perturbation protocol, ViT-Tiny + Attention Rollout attains Deletion AUC 0.211 against 0.432-0.525 for Swin-Tiny / ResNet18+CBAM / DenseNet121 + Grad-CAM (abs(Cohen's d) > 1.1), despite lower classification accuracy. Swin-Tiny disentangles architecture family from readout structure: despite being a Transformer, its spatial feature-map hierarchy makes it Grad-CAM compatible, showing that the operative factor is readout structure rather than architecture family. A model-agnostic control (RISE) compresses all families to Deletion AUC about 0.1, indicating the gap arises from the explainer pathway; notably, RISE outperforms all native methods, so native readout is a compatibility principle rather than an optimality guarantee. A blur-fill sensitivity analysis shows that the family ordering reverses under a different perturbation baseline, reinforcing that faithfulness rankings are joint properties of (model, explainer, perturbation operator) triples. An exploratory boundary-condition study on MVTec AD (pretrained models) indicates that audit results are dataset/task dependent and identifies conditions requiring qualification. The protocol yields actionable guidance: explanation pathways should be co-designed with model architectures based on readout structure, and deployed heatmaps should be accompanied by quantitative faithfulness metrics.

### [136] [Smooth Multi-Policy Causal Effect Estimation in Longitudinal Settings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14284)
*Wenxin Chen,Weishen Pan,Kyra Gan,Fei Wang*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为PEQ-Net的新方法，通过政策感知的重新参数化迭代条件期望（ICE）Q函数，实现多个动态治疗策略的联合估计。该方法利用共享的策略编码器和核均值嵌入来捕捉群体层面的策略差异，并在应用纵向目标最大似然估计（LTMLE）校正后，有效控制了二阶余项，降低了有限样本方差。实验表明，相较于现有基于ICE的方法，PEQ-Net在半合成数据上显著降低均方根误差，尤其在评估相近策略时表现更优。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统纵向因果推断方法对每个治疗策略单独估计，导致无法跨反事实信息共享，从而引入结构上不受控的二阶偏差，增加有限样本方差，即使使用标准的LTMLE去偏也难以解决此问题。

Method: 提出政策感知的ICE Q函数重参数化，构建基于共享策略编码器的Policy-Encoded Q Network（PEQ-Net），利用核均值嵌入学习策略间的群体差异表示，并结合LTMLE进行校正，以施加结构性约束于二阶余项。

Conclusion: PEQ-Net通过联合估计和结构约束设计，有效缓解了传统方法中的二阶偏差问题，为多策略比较提供了更稳健、高效的因果推断框架。

Abstract: Comparative evaluation of multiple dynamic treatment policies is essential for healthcare and policy decisions, yet conventional longitudinal causal inference methods estimate each in isolation, preventing information sharing across counterfactuals. We demonstrate that this separate estimation paradigm induces a structurally uncontrolled second-order bias, inflating finite-sample variance even after standard debiasing with longitudinal targeted maximum likelihood estimation(LTMLE). To address this, we propose a policy-aware reparameterization of Iterative Conditional Expectation (ICE) Q-functions that enables joint estimation through shared representations. We implement this approach in the Policy-Encoded Q Network (PEQ-Net), an architecture centered on a shared policy encoder. The encoder is trained using kernel mean embeddings, ensuring that the learned representation space reflects population-level policy dissimilarities. After applying an LTMLE correction step, we prove this design imposes a structural constraint on the second-order remainder, thereby stabilizing finite-sample variance. Experiments on semi-synthetic datasets demonstrate that PEQ-Net consistently outperforms existing ICE-based methods, achieving substantial reductions in root-mean-square error, particularly when evaluating closely related policies.

### [137] [Minimal-Intervention KV Retention: A Design-Space Study and a Diversity-Penalty Survivor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14292)
*Libo Sun,Po-wei Harn,Peixiong He,Xiao Qin*

TL;DR: 本文研究了在小预算下KV缓存压缩的七种机制，涵盖缓存表示、头级路由、压缩频率、解码行为和预算内评分等五个方面。在长形式数学推理任务（MATH-500）上，使用两个蒸馏推理模型（Qwen-7B 和 Llama-8B 变体）在预算 b ∈ {64, 128} 下测试，所有七种方法均被拒绝。随后提出 α：对 TriAttention 保留评分器的一次性修改，将 argmax-top-k 替换为受单一权重 λ 控制的 V 空间冗余惩罚的贪心设施选址选择。通过预注册协议在冻结开发集上调优 λ，验证集上确认结果；当 λ = 0.5 时，α 在两个 (模型, 预算) 组合中通过 Bonferroni 校正（Qwen b=128 与 Llama b=64），无显著负效应，预注册分支 A 触发。发现具有不对称性：最小评分修改胜过更复杂的结构重设计；而匹配内存、Sympy 评分、独立验证集的综合协议使该不对称性得以显现。

Result: 当 λ = 0.5 时，α 在两个 (模型, 预算) 组合中通过 Bonferroni 校正，未出现显著负效应，预注册分支 A 成功触发，表明其有效性。

Conclusion: 最小化的评分机制修改（α）在小预算下优于复杂结构重设计，且严格的预注册与独立验证协议是揭示此类不对称性的关键。

Abstract: KV-cache compression at small budgets is a crowded design space spanning cache representation, head-wise routing, compression cadence, decoding behavior, and within-budget scoring. All seven were rejected. We then propose $α$, a one-function modification to the TriAttention~\cite{mao2026triattention} retention scorer that replaces argmax-top-$k$ with greedy facility-location-inspired selection under a V-space redundancy penalty controlled by a single weight $λ$. A pre-registered protocol tunes $λ$ on a frozen development split and confirms on a disjoint held-out split; with $λ= 0.5$, $α$ clears Bonferroni on two of the four (model, budget) cells (Qwen $b{=}128$ and Llama $b{=}64$), no cell is significantly negative, and the pre-registered Branch~A triggers. The finding is asymmetric: a minimal scoring modification beat heavier structural redesigns in this regime, and the combined matched-memory, sympy-graded, held-out confirmation protocol is the evidence standard that made the asymmetry visible.

### [138] [Policy Optimization in Hybrid Discrete-Continuous Action Spaces via Mixed Gradients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14297)
*Matias Alvo,Daniel Russo,Yash Kanoria*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为混合策略优化（HPO）的新方法，用于处理混合离散-连续动作空间中的强化学习问题。该方法结合路径梯度和得分函数梯度，在保持无偏性的同时利用可微仿真，有效缓解了高维环境下的信用分配难题。实验表明，HPO在库存控制和切换线性二次调节器任务中显著优于PPO，且随着连续动作维度增加，性能差距扩大。此外，研究揭示了混合梯度的结构特性，发现交叉项在接近离散最优响应时趋于零，从而支持近似解耦更新以降低方差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准的无模型策略梯度方法在高维混合离散-连续动作空间中面临严重的信用分配问题，导致梯度质量差；而可微仿真在存在离散动作或非光滑动态时会产生有偏或无效梯度。因此需要一种既能利用可微性又可处理离散成分的方法。

Method: 提出混合策略优化（HPO），采用混合梯度估计器，结合路径梯度与得分函数梯度，在允许平滑性的区域通过反向传播进行优化，并保证梯度无偏。同时将具有动作不连续性的问题重新表述为混合形式，扩展其适用范围。

Result: HPO在库存控制和切换线性二次调节器任务中显著优于PPO，尤其在高维连续动作空间下优势更明显。分析显示，混合梯度中的交叉项在接近离散最优响应时趋于零，支持解耦更新并降低方差。

Conclusion: HPO是一种高效、可扩展的强化学习框架，适用于广泛存在的混合离散-连续动作结构，通过无偏混合梯度实现高质量优化，并具备理论支撑与实践优势。

Abstract: We study reinforcement learning in hybrid discrete-continuous action spaces, such as settings where the discrete component selects a regime (or index) and the continuous component optimizes within it -- a structure common in robotics, control, and operations problems. Standard model-free policy gradient methods rely on score-function (SF) estimators and suffer from severe credit-assignment issues in high-dimensional settings, leading to poor gradient quality. On the other hand, differentiable simulation largely sidesteps these issues by backpropagating through a simulator, but the presence of discrete actions or non-smooth dynamics yields biased or uninformative gradients. To address this, we propose Hybrid Policy Optimization (HPO), which backpropagates through the simulator wherever smoothness permits, using a mixed gradient estimator that combines pathwise and SF gradients while maintaining unbiasedness. We also show how problems with action discontinuities can be reformulated in hybrid form, further broadening its applicability. Empirically, HPO substantially outperforms PPO on inventory control and switched linear-quadratic regulator problems, with performance gaps increasing as the continuous action dimension grows. Finally, we characterize the structure of the mixed gradient, showing that its cross term -- which captures how continuous actions influence future discrete decisions -- becomes negligible near a discrete best response, thereby enabling approximate decentralized updates of the continuous and discrete components and reducing variance near optimality. All resources are available at github.com/MatiasAlvo/hybrid-rl.

</details>


### [139] [Language-Induced Priors for Domain Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14301)
*Qiyuan Chen,Jiayu Zhou,Raed Al Kontar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于语言描述的领域自适应方法，利用专家对目标领域的文本描述构建语言诱导先验（LIP），通过预训练大模型学习源域偏好，并结合期望最大化算法识别相关源域，适用于统计信号弱的情况。该框架在不同任务上均表现出色，理论证明其估计器接近最优冷启动均方误差，且不依赖先验质量仍具渐近一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当目标数据稀缺时，传统统计方法难以区分相关与无关源域，易导致负迁移；而专家提供的目标领域文本描述常被忽略，本文旨在利用此类语义信息缓解冷启动问题。

Method: 提出一种概率框架，将专家文本描述转化为语言诱导先验（LIP），利用预训练大模型生成偏好分布，并嵌入期望最大化算法以动态选择相关源域，兼容任何具有似然函数的参数化模型。

Result: 在高斯估计、C-MAPSS预测和MuJoCo运动控制三个任务上验证有效；理论分析表明，估计器在正确先验下接近最优冷启动均方误差，且无论先验质量如何，都保持渐近一致性。

Conclusion: 通过引入语言诱导先验，该框架有效缓解了冷启动条件下源域选择的难题，为少样本领域自适应提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: Domain adaptation faces a fundamental paradox in the cold-start regime. When target data is scarce, statistical methods fail to distinguish relevant source domains from irrelevant ones, which often leads to negative transfer. In this paper, we address this challenge by leveraging expert textual descriptions of the target domain, a resource that is often available but overlooked. We propose a probabilistic framework that translates these semantic descriptions into a choice model, namely a Language-Induced Prior (LIP), that learns the preferences from a pretrained Large Language Model (LLM). The LIP is then integrated into an Expectation-Maximization algorithm to identify source relevance. Methodologically, this framework is compatible with any parametric model where a likelihood is available. It allows the LIP to guide the selection of sources when target signals are weak, while gradually refining these choices as samples accumulate. Theoretically, we prove that the estimator roughly matches an oracle cold-start MSE under a correct prior, while remaining asymptotically consistent regardless of the quality of the LIP. Empirically, we validated the framework on a descriptive (Gaussian estimation), a predictive (C-MAPSS dataset), and a prescriptive task (MuJoCo hopper).
